dir=\"auto\"\u003eDeliver a constitution-compliant Smart Canteen workflow that captures menu plans per business window, routes submissions through approval, derives ingredient requirements, assigns suppliers, receives deliveries with quantity/weight/quality/price verification, and exposes analytics across the entire chain. Modules now include Administration \u0026amp; RBAC, planning, approval, aggregation, procurement, receiving, sales ingestion, and analytics—each exposing backend services, operator-facing consoles, data models keyed by \u003ccode\u003e(menu_date, canteen_id, meal_period)\u003c/code\u003e, and integration points for Smart Canteen sales/scales APIs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv with existing Smart Canteen backend services)\n\u003cstrong\u003ePrimary Dependencies\u003c/strong\u003e: NestJS REST framework, TypeORM for persistence, shared RBAC middleware, React 18 + Vite for operator consoles\n\u003cstrong\u003eStorage\u003c/strong\u003e: PostgreSQL (shared Smart Canteen cluster) hosting canonical ledger tables (\u003ccode\u003emenu_plan\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eingredient_requirement_line\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003epurchase_order\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ereceiving_record\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003esales_feed\u003c/code\u003e, analytics facts)\n\u003cstrong\u003eTesting\u003c/strong\u003e: Jest + Supertest for backend unit/contract testing, Playwright for key console flows; Pact-style contract tests for external APIs\n\u003cstrong\u003eTarget Platform\u003c/strong\u003e: Web backend services deployed on existing Linux containers plus internal React consoles; external clients integrate via REST APIs\n\u003cstrong\u003eProject Type\u003c/strong\u003e: Multi-tier web application (monorepo backend + frontend)\n\u003cstrong\u003ePerformance Goals\u003c/strong\u003e: Process ≥500 business windows/day; aggregation completes \u0026lt;60s/window; receiving-to-analytics lag \u0026lt;5 min; variance alerts \u0026lt;2 min.\n\u003cstrong\u003eConstraints\u003c/strong\u003e: Enforce deterministic state machines, append-only audit logs, capability permissions, and immutable receiving entries; analytics remains read-only.\n\u003cstrong\u003eScale/Scope\u003c/strong\u003e: Eight major modules, ~12 core entities, integrations with supplier master, manual sales import, and future IoT devices.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eConstitution Check\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca tables include \u003ccode\u003emenu_plan\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003emenu_submission\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003emenu_approval\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eingredient_requirement_list\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eingredient_requirement_line\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003esupplier_assignment\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003epurchase_order\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003epurchase_order_line\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ereceiving_record\u003c/code\u003e, and analytics fact tables. No spreadsheets or ad-hoc stores are allowed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRole-Isolated Accountability\u003c/strong\u003e: Capability-style permissions (PLAN_MENU, SUBMIT_MENU, APPROVE_MENU, VIEW_/MANAGE_INGREDIENT_AGGREGATION, MANAGE_PROCUREMENT, VIEW_PURCHASE_ORDERS, MANAGE_RECEIVING, VIEW_ANALYTICS) scoped by business window filters (canteen, meal period, optional date range).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDeterministic State Flow\u003c/strong\u003e: Draft → Submitted → Approved/Locked menus; approved menus emit aggregation views; procurement only acts on approved-derived lines; PO lines pending → received; PO issued → partially received → closed; analytics consumes posted states only; reopen operations require re-approval before downstream recompute.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClosed-Loop Supply Lifecycle\u003c/strong\u003e: Approved menus feed aggregation → supplier assignment → PO issuance → receiving; reopening menus invalidates derived layers; analytics ties menu through receiving and sales. Exceptions (inventory-sufficient, variance alerts) remain within ledger and notify upstream roles.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOperability \u0026amp; Insightful Concurrency\u003c/strong\u003e: Emit structured logs for each state change, metrics for window throughput, PO issuance, variance counts, and analytics freshness; set alerts for stuck states (\u0026gt;4h) and variance breaches; load-test planner/approver concurrency and 2k PO lines/day throughput.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" class="Box-sc-62in7e-0 lhfNqO js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Implementation Plan: Smart Canteen Menu-to-Procurement Flow</h1><a id="user-content-implementation-plan-smart-canteen-menu-to-procurement-flow" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Implementation Plan: Smart Canteen Menu-to-Procurement Flow" href="#implementation-plan-smart-canteen-menu-to-procurement-flow"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Branch</strong>: <code>001-canteen-supply</code> | <strong>Date</strong>: 2025-11-19 | <strong>Spec</strong>: <a href="/rocococococo/smart-canteen-project/blob/main/specs/001-canteen-supply/spec.md">specs/001-canteen-supply/spec.md</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Summary</h2><a id="user-content-summary" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Summary" href="#summary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Deliver a constitution-compliant Smart Canteen workflow that captures menu plans per business window, routes submissions through approval, derives ingredient requirements, assigns suppliers, receives deliveries with quantity/weight/quality/price verification, and exposes analytics across the entire chain. Modules now include Administration &amp; RBAC, planning, approval, aggregation, procurement, receiving, sales ingestion, and analytics—each exposing backend services, operator-facing consoles, data models keyed by <code>(menu_date, canteen_id, meal_period)</code>, and integration points for Smart Canteen sales/scales APIs.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Technical Context</h2><a id="user-content-technical-context" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Technical Context" href="#technical-context"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Language/Version</strong>: Node.js 20 LTS with TypeScript (aligned with existing Smart Canteen backend services)
<strong>Primary Dependencies</strong>: NestJS REST framework, TypeORM for persistence, shared RBAC middleware, React 18 + Vite for operator consoles
<strong>Storage</strong>: PostgreSQL (shared Smart Canteen cluster) hosting canonical ledger tables (<code>menu_plan</code>, <code>ingredient_requirement_line</code>, <code>purchase_order</code>, <code>receiving_record</code>, <code>sales_feed</code>, analytics facts)
<strong>Testing</strong>: Jest + Supertest for backend unit/contract testing, Playwright for key console flows; Pact-style contract tests for external APIs
<strong>Target Platform</strong>: Web backend services deployed on existing Linux containers plus internal React consoles; external clients integrate via REST APIs
<strong>Project Type</strong>: Multi-tier web application (monorepo backend + frontend)
<strong>Performance Goals</strong>: Process ≥500 business windows/day; aggregation completes &lt;60s/window; receiving-to-analytics lag &lt;5 min; variance alerts &lt;2 min.
<strong>Constraints</strong>: Enforce deterministic state machines, append-only audit logs, capability permissions, and immutable receiving entries; analytics remains read-only.
<strong>Scale/Scope</strong>: Eight major modules, ~12 core entities, integrations with supplier master, manual sales import, and future IoT devices.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Constitution Check</h2><a id="user-content-constitution-check" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Constitution Check" href="#constitution-check"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Chain-of-Record Integrity</strong>: Canonical tables include <code>menu_plan</code>, <code>menu_submission</code>, <code>menu_approval</code>, <code>ingredient_requirement_list</code>, <code>ingredient_requirement_line</code>, <code>supplier_assignment</code>, <code>purchase_order</code>, <code>purchase_order_line</code>, <code>receiving_record</code>, and analytics fact tables. No spreadsheets or ad-hoc stores are allowed.</li>
<li><strong>Role-Isolated Accountability</strong>: Capability-style permissions (PLAN_MENU, SUBMIT_MENU, APPROVE_MENU, VIEW_/MANAGE_INGREDIENT_AGGREGATION, MANAGE_PROCUREMENT, VIEW_PURCHASE_ORDERS, MANAGE_RECEIVING, VIEW_ANALYTICS) scoped by business window filters (canteen, meal period, optional date range).</li>
<li><strong>Deterministic State Flow</strong>: Draft → Submitted → Approved/Locked menus; approved menus emit aggregation views; procurement only acts on approved-derived lines; PO lines pending → received; PO issued → partially received → closed; analytics consumes posted states only; reopen operations require re-approval before downstream recompute.</li>
<li><strong>Closed-Loop Supply Lifecycle</strong>: Approved menus feed aggregation → supplier assignment → PO issuance → receiving; reopening menus invalidates derived layers; analytics ties menu through receiving and sales. Exceptions (inventory-sufficient, variance alerts) remain within ledger and notify upstream roles.</li>
<li><strong>Operability &amp; Insightful Concurrency</strong>: Emit structured logs for each state change, metrics for window throughput, PO issuance, variance counts, and analytics freshness; set alerts for stuck states (&gt;4h) and variance breaches; load-test planner/approver concurrency and 2k PO lines/day throughput.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Project Structure</h2><a id="user-content-project-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Project Structure" href="#project-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Documentation (feature-scoped)</h3><a id="user-content-documentation-feature-scoped" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Documentation (feature-scoped)" href="#documentation-feature-scoped"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Structure Decision</strong>: Single backend project with module directories under <code>src/</code>; frontend/operator consoles share existing web app but consume the same APIs. Tests organized by type to ensure menu→analytics chain coverage.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Module Implementation Strategy</h2><a id="user-content-module-implementation-strategy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Module Implementation Strategy" href="#module-implementation-strategy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Administration &amp; RBAC</h3><a id="user-content-1-administration--rbac" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Administration &amp; RBAC" href="#1-administration--rbac"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/admin/</code> manages users, roles, permission flags, and scope assignments; exposes APIs for role CRUD, scope filters, and permission audits while emitting events to the audit log stream whenever changes occur.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Admin console <code>/admin</code> where authorized personnel configure accounts, assign capability-style permissions (PLAN_MENU, MANAGE_RECEIVING, VIEW_ANALYTICS, etc.), and review scope coverage; includes change-review dialogs.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>role</code>, <code>permission_flag</code>, <code>role_permission</code>, <code>user_scope_mapping</code>, <code>scope_filter</code>, plus linkage to <code>audit_event</code> and notification templates for approvals/alerts.</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Notification service for broadcasting role/scope updates, centralized audit log sink, SSO/identity provider for user linkage.</li>
<li><em>This module enforces capability-style permissions and triggers audit logging whenever roles or scopes change, satisfying FR-Role-01..07.</em></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Menu Planning</h3><a id="user-content-2-menu-planning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Menu Planning" href="#2-menu-planning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/menu/</code> exposes draft CRUD, submission, and history APIs keyed by business window; enforces PLAN_MENU/SUBMIT_MENU scopes and stores ingredient remarks as immutable upstream context.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Planner console <code>/planning</code> allowing window selection, dish/ingredient editing, draft autosave, and read-only history lookup.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>menu_plan</code> (id, business_window fields, planner_id, status), <code>menu_plan_item</code> (dish refs, planned servings, notes), <code>menu_plan_ingredient</code> (ingredient, planned_quantity, unit, remark, dish linkage).</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Dish master catalog; optional template service for copying historical menus.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Menu Approval</h3><a id="user-content-3-menu-approval" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. Menu Approval" href="#3-menu-approval"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/approval/</code> consolidates submitted drafts, captures edits, emits <code>menu_approval</code> records, and handles reopen → reapprove flow; enforces APPROVE_MENU scopes per business window.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Reviewer workspace <code>/approval</code> with diffing, merge controls, and reopen actions.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>menu_submission</code>, <code>menu_approval</code> (snapshot JSON, approver_id, state), <code>menu_edit_log</code> recording deltas.</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Notification service to alert planners/procurement once approvals complete.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Ingredient Aggregation</h3><a id="user-content-4-ingredient-aggregation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Ingredient Aggregation" href="#4-ingredient-aggregation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/ingredients/</code> recomputes <code>ingredient_requirement_list/line</code> after approval, aggregates by ingredient+unit, persists lineage, and exposes state toggles (pending, ready, inventory-sufficient); only approved menus trigger recompute.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Operations view <code>/aggregation</code> to inspect demand; limited toggles for inventory-sufficient based on MANAGE_INGREDIENT_AGGREGATION permission.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>ingredient_requirement_list</code> (window_id, version, approved_menu_id), <code>ingredient_requirement_line</code> (ingredient_id, aggregated_quantity, unit, remark, source_ids, state_flags).</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Inventory service for sufficiency hints; event bus (e.g., message queue) to trigger recompute jobs.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Procurement &amp; Supplier Assignment</h3><a id="user-content-5-procurement--supplier-assignment" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Procurement &amp; Supplier Assignment" href="#5-procurement--supplier-assignment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/procurement/</code> allows selecting aggregated lines, assigning suppliers (one per line), and emitting purchase orders for each (window, supplier) pair; enforces MANAGE_PROCUREMENT/VIEW_PURCHASE_ORDERS.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Procurement UI <code>/procurement</code> with multi-select, supplier pickers, PO previews/downloads, and unassigned-line backlog.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>supplier_assignment</code>, <code>purchase_order</code> (window ref, supplier_id, status), <code>purchase_order_line</code> (reference to ingredient requirement line, inherited ingredient/unit/remark, planned quantity, state).</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Supplier master, outbound email/PDF dispatch, optional pricing catalogs.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. Receiving / Acceptance</h3><a id="user-content-6-receiving--acceptance" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. Receiving / Acceptance" href="#6-receiving--acceptance"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/receiving/</code> accepts actual quantity/weight, quality notes, photo uploads, and actual unit price per PO line; auto-computes variance, price deviation, actual amount, and exception flags; enforces MANAGE_RECEIVING/VIEW_RECEIVING.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Receiving console <code>/receiving</code> optimized for tablets, listing issued POs and per-line forms capturing the four verification dimensions in one step.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>receiving_record</code> (po_line_id, actual_quantity, actual_unit_price, actual_amount, quality_notes, photo_refs, variances, appended_by, appended_at), <code>po_line_state</code> (pending/received), PO status progression.</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Photo/object storage; variance alert notifications; future smart-scale/IoT connectors for automatic readings.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7. Sales Ingestion &amp; Feeds</h3><a id="user-content-7-sales-ingestion--feeds" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7. Sales Ingestion &amp; Feeds" href="#7-sales-ingestion--feeds"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/sales/</code> handles manual sales entry, CSV/Excel imports, and Smart Canteen sales/cashier API ingestion; validates entries against business windows and dishes, stores results in <code>sales_feed</code> and normalized <code>sales_entry</code> rows.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Sales console <code>/sales</code> enabling authorized staff to key in or import sales records, review validation errors, and override mismatched items while keeping audit history.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>sales_feed</code> (source, file metadata, status), <code>sales_entry</code> (business_window, dish_id, quantity, revenue, source_id, validation flags), plus join tables linking back to menu plan lines for lineage.</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Smart Canteen sales/cashier API, secure file upload pipeline, validation rulesets for dish/date matching, optional ETL scheduler.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">8. Analytics</h3><a id="user-content-8-analytics" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 8. Analytics" href="#8-analytics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backend module</strong>: <code>src/analytics/</code> builds read-only fact tables combining plan, aggregation, procurement, receiving, and sales feeds; serves APIs for plan-vs-sales, cost variance, supplier KPIs, export jobs, and saved analysis scenarios; enforces VIEW_ANALYTICS.</li>
<li><strong>Frontend entry</strong>: Analytics dashboard <code>/analytics</code> with tabular reports, export builder, saved filter sets, and placeholders for future visualization widgets.</li>
<li><strong>Data model</strong>: <code>analytics_fact_menu</code>, <code>analytics_fact_procurement</code>, <code>analytics_fact_receiving</code>, <code>analytics_fact_sales</code> (sourced from the Sales Ingestion module), derived views for plan_vs_sales, cost_variance, supplier_performance; all keyed by business window + entity ids.</li>
<li><strong>External dependencies</strong>: Sales ingestion APIs/feeds, Smart Canteen sales API, analytics export API for BI tools.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Complexity Tracking</h2><a id="user-content-complexity-tracking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Complexity Tracking" href="#complexity-tracking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
